LANG_ENG Parliament Does Not Support Amendment Freeing Tymoshenko
LANG_ENG Today , the Ukraine parliament dismissed , within the Code of Criminal Procedure amendment , the motion to revoke an article based on which the opposition leader , Yulia Tymoshenko , was sentenced .
LANG_ENG The amendment that would lead to freeing the imprisoned former Prime Minister was revoked during second reading of the proposal for mitigation of sentences for economic offences .
LANG_ENG In October , Tymoshenko was sentenced to seven years in prison for entering into what was reported to be a disadvantageous gas deal with Russia .
LANG_ENG The verdict is not yet final; the court will hear Tymoshenko &apos;s appeal in December .
LANG_ENG Tymoshenko claims the verdict is a political revenge of the regime; in the West , the trial has also evoked suspicion of being biased .
LANG_ENG The proposal to remove Article 365 from the Code of Criminal Procedure , upon which the former Prime Minister was sentenced , was supported by 147 members of parliament .
LANG_ENG Its ratification would require 226 votes .
LANG_ENG Libya &apos;s Victory
LANG_ENG The story of Libya &apos;s liberation , or rebellion , already has its defeated .
LANG_ENG Muammar Kaddafi is buried at an unknown place in the desert . Without him , the war is over .
LANG_ENG It is time to define the winners .
LANG_ENG As a rule , Islamists win in the country; the question is whether they are the moderate or the radical ones .
LANG_ENG The transitional cabinet declared itself a follower of the customary Sharia law , of which we have already heard .
LANG_ENG Libya will become a crime free country , as the punishment for stealing is having one &apos;s hand amputated .
LANG_ENG Women can forget about emancipation; potential religious renegades will be executed; etc .
LANG_ENG Instead of a dictator , a society consisting of competing tribes will be united by Koran .
LANG_ENG Libya will be in an order we cannot imagine and surely would not ask for .

LANG_ENG Their only excuse is that from their point of view , NATO raids were not controlled by an American general , but Allah , the greatness of whom they celebrated with each strike .

LANG_ENG It is quite likely that they will not . The West will then finally be able to boast about its selfless protection of human rights .
LANG_ENG Unless the followers of the Sharia law put a stop to that .
LANG_ENG New Era of Crisis Commences
LANG_ENG France and the rest of Europe are now in the investors &quot; spotlight .
LANG_ENG A statistical storm blew over Europe on Tuesday .
LANG_ENG Individual countries released their 3Q GDP data .
LANG_ENG Between quarters , the Czech economy stagnated; Germany and France are growing .
LANG_ENG Yet the debit market is breaking records today .
LANG_ENG Investors are no longer looking at only Italy; they now focus on Spain , France , Austria , and others .
LANG_ENG Eurozone statistical offices in Germany , Czech Republic , and some other countries , released their preliminary estimates of economic development in the third quarter .
LANG_ENG Germany &apos;s GDP has grown by the expected 0.5%; and France &apos;s by 0.4% .
LANG_ENG Both countries also adjusted their second quarter data , where Germany did better than expected (a 0.3% increase instead of the original 0.1%). France reported a slight decrease , by 0.1% (the original information suggested stagnation).
LANG_ENG In this year &apos;s third quarter , the Czech economy showed an interim increase of 1.5% .
LANG_ENG Between the quarters though , the GDP stagnated . According to the Czech Statistical Office , this confirmed the trend of a gradual slowing of economic growth .
LANG_ENG The results are worse than estimates by analysts .
LANG_ENG Key events:
LANG_ENG In this year &apos;s third quarter , Czech economy showed an interim increase of 1.5%; however , it stagnated between the quarters .
LANG_ENG Based on preliminary and seasonal data , in the third quarter , the German economy grew by 0.5% .
LANG_ENG Between July and September , the economy of both the Eurozone and the European Union grew , compared to the previous quarter , by 0.2% , which corresponds with estimates by analysts .
LANG_ENG The Greek economy showed an interim decrease of 5.2% .
LANG_ENG The earnings on its 10-year bonds are 28.45% .
LANG_ENG Earnings of both Italian and Spanish bonds are growing towards critical limits .
LANG_ENG Even Austria , Netherlands , France , and Belgium , etc. are beginning to experience problems .
LANG_ENG Despite the fact that the situation in the region is getting worse , earnings of Czech 1 - year bonds stay under 4% .
LANG_ENG Voices are coming from Germany , suggesting that ECB be the last resort creditor .
LANG_ENG Czechs qualified for EURO .
LANG_ENG In Montenegro they won 1: 0 and celebrate a 200 million windfall .
LANG_ENG Football representation successfully managed the toughest task of the season !
LANG_ENG Thanks to both the great Čech and beautiful goal of Petr Jiráček , they won 1: 0 .
LANG_ENG In the second half , Czech football was lucky to maintain its luxury lead from the home return match , and will again feature at the European Championship .
LANG_ENG IHNED.cz watched the progress match in a detailed report .
LANG_ENG Nearly no excitement in the first half , and a great portion of luck in the other .
LANG_ENG Czech representation team , partially due to the home team &apos;s failure in the close; the great Čech; and heroic Jiráček; won 1: 0 in Montenegro , and celebrates moving on to the European Championship .
LANG_ENG Perfect Czech team defence only allowed the Montenegro team to threaten in the second half .
LANG_ENG Damjanovic and Vucinic became the match &apos;s least lucky couple after losing two great opportunities .
LANG_ENG The wonderful Petr Čech is one of the reasons the Czech representation team will not miss the next year &apos;s European Championship . And Czech football will thus gain nearly 200 million Czech Crowns .
LANG_ENG From the opening minutes , the game was very pugnacious .
LANG_ENG Both teams found it difficult to join in the combination; the game remained around the mid-field line most of the time .
LANG_ENG That was also why there was no pressure from the home team in the first half . Long kicks behind the defence were neatly averted by the Czech defence .
LANG_ENG Iranian Students Are Prepared to Die for Their Country &apos;s Nuclear Program
LANG_ENG They created a live shield .
LANG_ENG Several hundred university students created a live chain around the nuclear power plant in Iran .
LANG_ENG The gesture is to express their support of their country &apos;s nuclear program against a possible Israel attack .
LANG_ENG At Tuesday noon , students &apos; prayers in front of the building were followed by their chanting of death to both the USA and Israel .
LANG_ENG In Isfahan , Iran , several hundred university students created a live chain around Isfahan Uranium Conversion Facility .
LANG_ENG This way , they express their readiness to protect their country &apos;s nuclear program with their own lives .
LANG_ENG In its recent report , the International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA) stated that everything leads to the conclusion that Iran has not stopped striving for a nuclear weapon .
LANG_ENG Possible attack on Iran nuclear facilities has been discussed in Israel .
LANG_ENG At Tuesday noon , students &apos; prayers in front of the entrance into Isfahan Uranium Conversion Facility were followed by their chanting of death to both the USA and Israel .
LANG_ENG In case of an attack , aimed at the highest possible paralysation of the Iranian nuclear program , the targets would be , based on Israel press , the facilities in both Isfahan and Natanz , where the uranium is being enriched .
LANG_ENG An Obese Child &apos;s Diet: No breakfast and sausage for dinner
LANG_ENG Over a third of children between 9 and 13 are overweight; while 9% of schoolchildren are overweight , 5% are obese .
LANG_ENG As a recent research shows , obese children usually come from families with unhealthy lifestyle .
LANG_ENG Again , we can see the importance of the environment and models surrounding a human being for his or her healthy development .
LANG_ENG For example , sausages occur up to half more frequently on the tables of obese children compared to the families of children with standard weight .
LANG_ENG Over 19% of obese children had fried chips for dinner the day before the research connected to the educational event called Obesity is No Accident .
LANG_ENG Moreover , the families of obese children do not practise sports . However , this concerns a majority of families of current schoolchildren - only 15% of the children said their parents find time for sports activities at least once a week .
LANG_ENG The research was performed among 900 children .
LANG_ENG The research took place at the end of last year &apos;s school year; it included almost 900 elementary school children from throughout Bohemia .
LANG_ENG It was the second year of the Obesity is No Accident event supported by both Všeobecná zdravotní pojišťovna insurance company and Unilever .
LANG_ENG So far , the project has been joined by over 12 thousand school children from 4th to 8th grades .
LANG_ENG Proper diet and sufficient sports activities represent key defining factors causing dramatically growing number of children who are either overweight or obese .
LANG_ENG &quot; For example , only half of those inquired said they have five meals a day , in the breakfast-snack-lunch-snack-dinner pattern , one of the basic preconditions of correct diet , &quot; one of the results of the research says .
LANG_ENG No lunch and sausage in the evening
LANG_ENG Experts warn that even relative details are crucial for healthy development; such as a regular time of family breakfast .
LANG_ENG In the Czech Republic , only 23% of schoolchildren &apos;s families have breakfast together .
LANG_ENG In a majority of families , everyone has breakfast separately .
LANG_ENG The worst discovery was the fact that in one tenth of households people do not have breakfast at all .
LANG_ENG Yet breakfast is the core of proper daily diet .
LANG_ENG A survey has shown that fries are consumed more often in the families of obese children .
LANG_ENG Nearly everyone - regardless of their weight - drinks sweet soft drinks every day (70%).
LANG_ENG Though over 40% of children do sports regularly , the number drops down to less than a half - 15% - when it comes to their parents .
LANG_ENG Compose your own menu
LANG_ENG Another part of the survey allowed selected children (204 boys and 172 girls from 13 schools) to compose their own menu based on selection offered and their taste and opinions .
LANG_ENG &quot; Diet preferences of Czech children between 12 and 15 are far from ideal as regards healthy diet . &quot;
LANG_ENG Their favourite meals include large number of flour , meat , and sweet dishes .
LANG_ENG &quot; Especially alarming is the high popularity of sweet soft drinks , &quot; the final report of the survey concludes .
LANG_ENG As the main dish for lunch , pasta won very tightly over poultry .
LANG_ENG However , children showed very little interest in legumes , fish , and vegetable lunches .
LANG_ENG Tendency towards health
LANG_ENG The survey also showed that children are willing to adjust their eating habits provided they are given correct information .
LANG_ENG &quot; Many participants from the survey control group showed a significant shift of preferences towards healthy food when completing a questionnaire after the end of the Obesity is No Accident educational lecture , &quot; project results show .
LANG_ENG This was quite significant , for example , in case of sweet soft drinks , where more children would begin to prefer plain water .
LANG_ENG In addition , for their main course , children ticked poultry and fish more often , limiting sweet meals and dumplings .
LANG_ENG A Stylist Must Also Be a Good Psychologist , Professionals Claim
LANG_ENG In the opening article on stylist training , I was complaining a bit about the amount of information in the introductory lessons .
LANG_ENG I had no idea what was coming .
LANG_ENG Lectures by three experts from the field; dressing tips for difficult figures; and a seminar on how it works in practise .
LANG_ENG And more is yet to come .
LANG_ENG The closer we get to the final exam , the more information and practical tasks await .
LANG_ENG The training takes place every Saturday and Sunday , but it is really packed with information .
LANG_ENG This time , together with Alenka , the Director , (there is not a single man in the course) we discussed how to dress a woman whose body is not in perfect symmetry .
LANG_ENG A majority of women are not perfectly symmetrical .
LANG_ENG One has a short neck , the other has a boyish figure without proper curves , yet another is overweight .
LANG_ENG A stylist must know how to optically soften wide shoulders , make the neck look longer , or add the curves necessary .
LANG_ENG We were given tips on how to accentuate the figure of women such as Jennifer Lopez , i.e. with bigger breasts and hips and narrow waist , and not to dress them too provocatively .
LANG_ENG For example , if the difference between the waist and hips is such that the skirt or trousers do not fit , it is worth to have at least one piece custom-made .
LANG_ENG You will definitely not regret the investment , as perfectly fitting clothes are priceless .
LANG_ENG In a custom-made skirt , you will feel much better than in one that keeps shifting , rolling up , sticking out in your waist , etc .
LANG_ENG Boyish figures , on the other hand , can wear clothes with ruffling , appliqué , embroidery , or shirring .
LANG_ENG Given the abundance of such information and figure types , I am glad to have a whole week to sort it all out in my head .
LANG_ENG Still , I fear it is too much , with regard to the homework we were given .
LANG_ENG Each of the course participants was given a celebrity to create two outfits for: day and night .
LANG_ENG We must consider their current appearance , their fashion style , and figure type .
LANG_ENG I am to dress Miranda Kerr whom you may know from the Victoria &apos;s Secret campaigns .
LANG_ENG Inside I rejoice , as she is so much easier to dress than , say , Britney Spears , Christina Aguilera , who has recently gained about a ton (please , understand I am exaggerating), or the very young Selena Gomez .
LANG_ENG We must cut the clothes out of magazines or find them on the Internet and print and graphically process them .
LANG_ENG Moodboard , as the result is called , then expresses our personal style and attitude to graphic depiction .
LANG_ENG It is important to think about the graphic part of styling .
LANG_ENG A stylist does not just dress physical people , but creates product pages in magazines (based on specific instructions , for example , trendy purses , coats , etc .).
LANG_ENG This is what a stylist and designer , Mario Kameník , was telling us about .
LANG_ENG But that was not until Sunday .
LANG_ENG A stylist needs general knowledge
LANG_ENG Saturday &apos;s lecture , filled with information on figure types , was livened up by three guests from the field .
LANG_ENG A stylist , Honza Pokorný; a fashion designer , Jakub Polanka; and a fashion photographer , Ben Renč .
LANG_ENG Jakub reminded us that fashion is an illusion , and a stylist should be able to use this fact .
LANG_ENG A good stylist can work with a single piece of clothing in different ways .
LANG_ENG In this case , variability is key .
LANG_ENG For example , a trench coat may be worn in the standard way , over jeans and T-shirt , as a coat; but it may also be worn on naked body , with step-ins , as a dress .
LANG_ENG Another option is rolling up the sleeves or collar , and the entire look changes completely .
LANG_ENG &quot; Play with it , &quot; he emphasised .
LANG_ENG However , I appreciated the following advice the most: &quot; For your work , you need to know the rules perfectly . &quot;
LANG_ENG &apos;Then you can start breaking them , &apos; Jakub told us .
LANG_ENG Here I finally understood why we drill all the definitions and rules of what to combine with what and why , while in fashion magazines we often see something else .
LANG_ENG Not to mention fashion shows .
LANG_ENG From Ben , the photographer , I learned that a stylist must have more outfit versions prepared than the number he is to take pictures of .
LANG_ENG So , for a ten-page fashion story (equals ten outfits), I have to be ready to create at least fifteen of them .
LANG_ENG Now I also know that in the picture , a piece of clothing often looks and functions in combination with others completely different from reality .
LANG_ENG We must therefore take that into consideration when creating an outfit .
LANG_ENG Honza Pokorný confirmed that image and style often are half the success .
LANG_ENG Just look at Madonna , who is no miraculous singer , yet her image and marketing turned her into a worldwide star .
LANG_ENG The attitude towards stylist services is still rather cold in the Czech Republic .
LANG_ENG Even famous people often consider it redundant (believing it is sufficient to be good at something , and how they look at it comes second).
LANG_ENG And if someone finally lets us create their styling , then we should expect them to give us different (smaller) size than what they really wear .
LANG_ENG Then , we are left to Google and find out if the tabloids wrote something about a celebrity gaining / losing weight , etc .
LANG_ENG On Sunday , both Honza and Mario were stressing the fact that for a stylist it is not enough to know about fashion and be able to create an outfit .
LANG_ENG Our work chiefly consists of communicating with people we dress; it is therefore important to be a good psychologist .
LANG_ENG To be able to estimate people , not to pander , and stick to one &apos;s opinion .
LANG_ENG &quot; If a manager asks you to go through her clothes and add some nice pieces , you cannot throw out her entire wardrobe telling her how awful the clothes are . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; Find at least a few pieces you can praise , and recommend what to wear them with &quot; Mario says .
LANG_ENG He also showed us what specifically a duty bag must contain .
LANG_ENG That is the bag you fasten around your waist to carry all the props you need .
LANG_ENG Aside from the obvious things , such as scissors , a sticky roller , or safety pins , it should have a nylon thread (for the stylist to use when taking pictures of products such as purses or hats), special clip-ons for holding the clothes in the back in case it is too large (pins and similar things are forbidden as they damage the clothes), or a sewing set .
LANG_ENG To have some change from listening , and gain some practical experience , we learned how to properly underlay shoe soles .
LANG_ENG Even when taking photographs in a studio where the surface is even , the soles might get damaged - not to mention shooting outside .
LANG_ENG And so we were sticking away .
LANG_ENG You must not touch the shoes with the scissors , to avoid any damage .
LANG_ENG This requires real skill .
LANG_ENG Mario pleased me by praising my job .
LANG_ENG The skills mentioned are really not my cup of tea .
LANG_ENG This is just a fragment of what we heard during the second weekend course session .
LANG_ENG I am beginning to realise that to be a professional stylist is no piece of cake , no matter what people say .
LANG_ENG V Need for Speed: The Run takes place across America .
LANG_ENG Review
LANG_ENG An originally carefree ride turned into a routine morning drive to work because of a series of completely superfluous and sloppy mistakes .
LANG_ENG The ambitions were met to a certain point , but it does not matter since nobody obviously wanted to do any extra work .
LANG_ENG Before it was released , the new version subtitled The Run created high expectations .
LANG_ENG It promised to shift the old Need For Speed racing series in a new direction; the demos made it look like a game that might stand up in the action racing genre .
LANG_ENG We were curious to see the sections where the main character gets out of the car and runs .
LANG_ENG Typical for the NFS series though , in the end many things are different from what we expected .
LANG_ENG The game represents a possibly decent arcade race , but the whole is burdened by several unnecessary mistakes featured in the series for a number of years .
LANG_ENG This means they are not really mistakes , but the expression of an incomprehensible laziness of the developers .
LANG_ENG The adventure opens very well .
LANG_ENG You are introduced into a story , where the main character , Jack , decides to solve some personal issues by participating in an illegal race across America .
LANG_ENG You get in the car on the west coast , in San Francisco , and your task is to be the first one to reach New York .
LANG_ENG The idea brings several interesting features .
LANG_ENG The route is divided into ten stages , subdivided into over fifty races .
LANG_ENG This means each race takes place on a different route , and given stages are set in varied and interesting environments .
LANG_ENG One thus does not feel the game keeps offering the same things .
LANG_ENG Despite the graphics being on the same level of previous parts of the series , some of the environments are very nice to look at .
LANG_ENG Still , it is nothing world-shattering .
LANG_ENG Driving through the desert , autumnal countryside , or high in snow-covered mountains is visually very pleasant though .
LANG_ENG In addition , the races are , from time to time , enlivened by an untypical feature .
LANG_ENG For example , in the desert , you get into a sandstorm , significantly decreasing the visibility .
LANG_ENG On the other hand , in the mountains , you have to be careful not to get under an avalanche .
LANG_ENG Individual races are ordered fairly well .
LANG_ENG There are just a few types , but it is sufficient .
LANG_ENG For a while , you try to overtake a number of competitors (basically a regular race); then you try to beat the time (standard stopwatch race); or you are in a duel with a single rival .
LANG_ENG On top of everything else you sometimes come across the police who make your efforts more difficult .
LANG_ENG The parts outside the car are new .
LANG_ENG They are just interactive animations , where most of the time Jack is running away from someone and you need to help him by pressing the right buttons at the right time .
LANG_ENG Nothing difficult .
LANG_ENG It is a surprise though , that these parts are much less in number than you would expect (just three to be precise).
LANG_ENG It actually turns out to be good for the game , because this feature does not get to be boring; within what was already said , it is one of the things that make the game more entertaining .
LANG_ENG The driving model follows the footsteps of the previous parts .
LANG_ENG This means that it is nothing special anymore , but it cannot be considered a negative .
LANG_ENG If you are looking for a real-to-life simulation , you will have to look elsewhere .
LANG_ENG Still , this driving model is fully suitable for the action style racing , even though we could find better at the competition .
LANG_ENG So far , everything is just right .
LANG_ENG However , after some time , problems come .
LANG_ENG In contrast with the driving model , the collision model is not that good .
LANG_ENG From a game of this type , one does not expect complicated deformations and collisions , but when you have no idea , before crashing into any object , how your car will act , something is not right .
LANG_ENG Typically , when overtaking or passing cars tightly in common traffic , you sometimes lightly touch the other car . Yet sometimes in nearly identical situation your car ends up in wild pirouettes .
LANG_ENG Or , crashed completely .
LANG_ENG This is not such a big deal due to the restart system , but is enough to spoil the fun .
LANG_ENG The restarts are done so that if you crash or get far off the track , the game takes you back to the last interrupted point .
LANG_ENG Nevertheless , there are only five restarts available per each race .
LANG_ENG If you use them up , you have to start the race from the beginning .
LANG_ENG This makes it an aid in case something does not work out , but you cannot rely on it completely .
LANG_ENG Sometimes the restarts are not enough and you need to learn a given section of the race by heart .
LANG_ENG A significant shortcoming of the game is the fact that the same things often happen in the same places .
LANG_ENG For example , some turns have to be driven through in a specific way , otherwise you simply do not fit in .
LANG_ENG At other times you meet civilian cars at a given place in the very same configuration , no matter if you come first , fifth , five seconds earlier , or one minute later .
LANG_ENG This is especially annoying in situations where you can see how your rival drives through the two cars coming in the opposite direction so easily , while when you get there , the cars are already positioned so that you have to either drive around or slow down .
LANG_ENG It makes no difference when you get to them; everything is set so that the situation always occurs just in front of your nose .
LANG_ENG The competitors have other advantages , too .
LANG_ENG While playing the game , you find several places , where , regardless of time , the same competitor overtakes you at the very same spot .
LANG_ENG This is most obvious at the end of the game , on a long bridge , where you are driving in the opposite direction .
LANG_ENG Obviously , your rival has to get in front of you no matter what .
LANG_ENG The thing is that when he is driving in front of you , he makes your vision worse , which causes you to crash the car a few times in the section .
LANG_ENG One can understand the attempt at making the game more interesting and adrenalin-filled , but it is so obvious it gets annoying quickly .
LANG_ENG It &apos;s a pity , because despite the simple driving model , the game is entertaining and sometimes even so full of action you do not have time to pay attention to what is happening around you .
LANG_ENG It is not important whether the reason you do not get bored is the concept with fifty unique tracks , ordering of races , or something else .
LANG_ENG The idea of changing cars during races is unusual .
LANG_ENG You have to watch out for gas stations along the way , as that is where you car may change despite the fact that in most of the cases the one you have is fully sufficient .
LANG_ENG Cars are divided into three categories .
LANG_ENG Sports cars are suitable for cities; strong American cars for straight highway sections; and exotic supersports cars for technical driving , such as along crooked mountain tracks .
LANG_ENG The key story mode is closely connected with the challenge mode; these are the races in individual locations you know from the story .
LANG_ENG Here , you gain both medals and experience points for your profile , common for both challenges and the story .
LANG_ENG Various features unlock fir getting a higher driver level: starting with cars and ending with profile backgrounds .
LANG_ENG Again , the profile is interconnected with an on-line Autolog function , which , among other things , compares the results you have reached with those of other players , and ensures community functions .
LANG_ENG Yet another setback difficult to understand; is the situation from the last race in the story .
LANG_ENG You and your car get into a subway tunnel (let &apos;s say you do), where you speed down the tracks in the darkness (let &apos;s say you do).
LANG_ENG Your speedometer shows numbers from 150 to 200 km / h (let &apos;s say it does), when suddenly , a subway train comes running down from behind you , turning your car into a pile of scrap metal .
LANG_ENG For several days , our editorial staff kept discussing whether when designing the game no one thought for a moment or whether its authors really think we are such morons .
LANG_ENG The technical part of the game is nothing extraordinary; but the overall visual impression is mostly pleasant , sometimes even great .
LANG_ENG It is a pity though , that in some dramatic moments , the recording , in some cases rather tragically , decreases .
LANG_ENG This especially concerns accidents with large number of participants , where fluent recoding would not help you much anyway .
LANG_ENG The sound is all right; the soundtrack is a matter of taste .
LANG_ENG In order to please the widest possible young audience , the soundtrack is &apos; flecked in from all quarters &apos;; but there probably will not be many people buying the game because of its music .
LANG_ENG Overall impression of Need for Speed: The Run is quite confused .
LANG_ENG If the game avoided those clearly redundant mistakes , we could sincerely say that The Run is the best part of NFS for the past several years .
LANG_ENG However , the game feels unfinished .
LANG_ENG It surely is a nice entertainment , but prepare to be blinded by the mistakes with the strength of airport spotlights .

LANG_ENG EU Ambassadress Vicenová:
LANG_ENG Czechs have the reputation of being negative and euro-sceptical
LANG_ENG &quot; Lisbon Treaty caused significant imbalance between individual institutions . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; I did not expect it to be such a tough war . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; It will take five or six years before the situation becomes somewhat stable , calm , and before all players get used to their new roles , &quot; EU Ambassadress Milena Vicenová opened her lecture at the Law Department sharply .
LANG_ENG She proved how true she is to her &quot; Clearly and openly about Europe &quot; motto in the very first part of her lecture , where she described individual EU organs and the relationships between them in such a clear and intelligible , way that many lecturers from the UK Law Dept. could be jealous .
LANG_ENG Moreover , Vicenová praised the work of new long-term President of the European Council , Herman Van Rompuy:
LANG_ENG &quot; At first , critics said he was plain , a grey office mouse who cannot fulfil any roles; I have to say everyone was amazed at how wonderfully he acquitted his role . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; He is a person who can listen to all twenty-seven member states , communicate with them perfectly , and who has a clear vision of where the EU should be headed . &quot;
LANG_ENG She explained her new position of foreign affairs and security policy representative as a reply to a question: &quot; Who is the European Union ? Which phone number should I call ? &quot;; i.e. as an important step to unification and better clarity of Union &apos;s policy towards countries such as China or India .
LANG_ENG No One Wants To Ban Our Cheese Specialties
LANG_ENG Vicenová further focused on the agenda crucial for the EU in the past , present , and near future .
LANG_ENG She described Czech presidency from the year before last as a success .
LANG_ENG Czechs were dealing with the coming financial crisis; they solved the as crisis; and organised the East Partnership Summit .
LANG_ENG She said the fall of the government at the time was a great negative causing significant damage to the Czech Republic .
LANG_ENG Currently , Czech representatives in the EU has been very busy .
LANG_ENG As the ambassadress said , both the presidency and the following financial crisis caused an ongoing stirring .
LANG_ENG In addition , a new seven-year EU budget needs to be passed , which is very complicated due to the current crisis .

LANG_ENG &quot; I really do not like all the abbreviations , foreign words , and jargon no one understands .

LANG_ENG In this regard , she appreciated the roles of both the Czech Republic and Herman Van Rompuy in pushing forward the rule based on which , all topics influencing the entire EU should be negotiated by all member states , and not just those belonging into the Eurozone .
LANG_ENG Brand Story:
LANG_ENG The IMB Innovator Starts the Second Century of Its Existence
LANG_ENG Should someone search for the word that would best express the IMB strategy , the closest one would probably be &quot; long-term . &quot;
LANG_ENG To the wide public , IMB is a symbol of technological revolution; the company is seen as a highly temporary one , yet it was founded over a hundred years ago .
LANG_ENG The company &apos;s durability goes back to its first boss , a visionary , Thomas J. Watson Sr.
LANG_ENG He believed in his motto saying that numerous world problems can be easily solved if people are willing to think .
LANG_ENG His motto: &apos; Think ! &apos; thus become an imprint around which the life of the future giant would unfold (as well as the name of its internal magazine that IMB started to publish in 1935).
LANG_ENG Moreover , it was the foundation of company culture Watson was building carefully .
LANG_ENG &quot; For us in IMB , long-term thinking means continuous movement towards the future .
LANG_ENG IMB survived and flourished for a hundred years , because it remained true to its original values , while it was not afraid to change everything around itself .
LANG_ENG During our first century , this allowed us to transform the technology , business , and the company .
LANG_ENG In the second century , we hope to be able to achieve even more , &quot; says current company Director , Samuel J. Palmisano , on the occasion of the anniversary .
LANG_ENG Sophisticated System
LANG_ENG In the 1930s , Watson approached employee care similarly to Baťa in the Czech Republic - people from IMB were among the first American employees to have a paid holiday , insurance from their employer , an elegant uniform , and a sophisticated system of bonuses for the best inventors and businessmen .
LANG_ENG Just as sophisticated is IBM &apos;s long-term relationship with customers .
LANG_ENG From the very beginning , the company was brilliant in exploiting talented people . It was one of the first world companies to abolish all discrimination , which rendered it with great selection .
LANG_ENG Consistent with the anti-discrimination strategy is the current plan expecting a woman , Virginia Rometty , to take over after Palmisano next year .
LANG_ENG She has been working in IMB for thirty years; she is currently a Director of Sales , Marketing , and Strategy .
LANG_ENG In the last few years , IMB has been organising jams , on-line brainstorming sessions , from which many future strategies and innovations arise .
LANG_ENG It is no surprise that the ideas are plentiful - the company employs nearly half a million people .
LANG_ENG Institution with a Good Reputation
LANG_ENG Company &apos;s strong business position is ensured by its strong internal and external image .
LANG_ENG &quot; From the beginning , the concept of IBM was that of an institution rather than a technology company , &apos; a Harvard Business School Professor and author of a book about IBM , Rosabeth Moss Kanter , told the Economist .
LANG_ENG &quot; IBM is not a technology firm; it is a company that helps to solve business problems using technology , &quot; George Colony of Forrester Research consultation company adds .
LANG_ENG As the company itself says , there is a difference between entering a market and creating it .
LANG_ENG During the hundred years , IMB , or the &quot; Big Blue , &quot; as it is called in the US because of its logo , has grown into one of the largest companies in the world .
LANG_ENG It seems to be the most universal technology company - developing hardware and software; infrastructure; hosting; and consultation services within a range from servers to nanotechnologies .
LANG_ENG It holds the most patents of all American technology companies; five of its employees were awarded the Nobel Price .
LANG_ENG Its inventions include , for example , the cash point , pay card , financial swap , bar code , and floppy disc .
LANG_ENG With about 220 billion dollars , based on market capitalisation , IBM has become the second largest technology company (Apple being number one) this year , overrunning Microsoft for the first time since 1996 .
LANG_ENG View Ahead
LANG_ENG Not all of its products fitted the taste of both the customers and period . For example , IBM failed with its own operating system OS / 2; Prodigy on-line services; and IBM PCjr computers .
LANG_ENG &quot; If your business is defined by movement forward , you cannot be emotionally attached to the past , &apos; says Samuel J. Palmisano .
LANG_ENG That is why IBM easily builds its foundations on many platforms - if they do not work , it leaves them .
LANG_ENG This is how it differs from , for example , its competitor , Microsoft , which basically stands and falls on Windows , its operating system .
LANG_ENG Perspective Technology
LANG_ENG IBM &apos;s revenues chiefly consist of services , about one fifth for each comes from software and hardware .
LANG_ENG While in 1990 , with over a half share , it was the strongest hardware representative .
LANG_ENG Since 2000 , IBM has sold low profitable assets worth 15 billion dollars . During the same time , it has invested 58 billion dollars into purchasing of perspective technologies .
LANG_ENG It has continued the investments even after 2008 , when the modern economic crisis first hit the world .
LANG_ENG IBM follows the legacy of its first director , Thomas J. Watson , who increased the amount of investments during the Great Depression .
LANG_ENG So far , IMB seems to be getting through the current crisis without any harm .
LANG_ENG Since the beginning of 2008 , the price of IBM &apos;s shares has grown by remarkable 120 per cent; company &apos;s net earnings have been growing continuously .
LANG_ENG IBM &apos;s company motto is to change everything , except for its values .
LANG_ENG We may therefore expect that even if another crisis comes , this flexible giant will manage .
LANG_ENG IBM History: From Cheese Cutter To Space Travel
LANG_ENG IBM (International Business Machines) was founded in New York , a hundred years ago . Its original name &quot; Computing Tabulating Recording Corporation &quot; was quite complicated .
LANG_ENG It took the name of IBM in 1924 . Originally , this was a brand used for company &apos;s branches in Canada and South America .
LANG_ENG Foundations for the later IBM were laid by a merger of four companies , the history of which goes back to the 1880s .
LANG_ENG They owned technologies such as the legendary &quot; time clock , &quot; i.e. a clock recording the time when employees arrive and leave work .
LANG_ENG The architect of the new company was a businessman , Charles Ranlett Flint , who , until 1930 , also presided over the company &apos;s Board of Trustees .
LANG_ENG Flint hired a director of a competing company , Thomas J. Watson , to help him with company management .
LANG_ENG The leader then put the IBM &apos;s founder in the shade - Watson &apos;s ideas remain the base for invincible company culture and identity .
LANG_ENG Watson led the company until 1952 .
LANG_ENG IBM , as its name suggests , started by producing and selling various business machines - from meat and cheese cutters to cash registers .
LANG_ENG During the first four years of Watson &apos;s leadership , the revenue doubled to nine million dollars , and company &apos;s vast expansion into all continents commenced .
LANG_ENG Watson became so essential for the company , that after nearly forty years , his position in the director &apos;s chair was taken by his son , Thomas Watson Junior .
LANG_ENG Under his leadership , IBM started to develop artificial intelligence and created the first programming language .
LANG_ENG In 1960s , both people and computers from IBM helped NASA control space flights - to Mercury , Saturn , and in 1969 , man &apos;s flight to the Moon .
LANG_ENG Meanwhile , in 1964 , IBM developed the first computer family - the IBM line System / 360 .
LANG_ENG The classic PC that defined the computer standards of the period , called IBM 5150 , came to the market in 1981 .
LANG_ENG Twenty years later , IBM sold computer production to a Chinese company , Lenovo , While buying the consultant division of PricewaterhouseCoopers , and thus commenced its full focus on consulting and high added value services .
LANG_ENG In the past three years , IBM has been highly successful with its Smarter Planet concept .
LANG_ENG Its goal is both smart exploitation of technologies in areas that have not yet been planned for and improving the situation in traffic or town management .
LANG_ENG For commerce , IBM has recently introduced a Smarter Commerce platform that helps businessmen control the whole commerce cycle .
LANG_ENG IBM &apos;s history is strong even in our country .
LANG_ENG In former Czechoslovakia , as the first country in both Central and Eastern Europe , IBM founded its branch in 1932 .
LANG_ENG Today , IBM CZ also runs a strategic outsourcing centre in Brno .
LANG_ENG The headquarters for both Central and Eastern Europe resides in Prague , where there also is a world level research team focusing on voice recognition .

LANG_ENG Iveto , keep the fool , I don &apos;t want him anymore !

LANG_ENG &quot; We don &apos;t sleep together , and I don &apos;t care where she goes , with whom , and if she has a boyfriend .
LANG_ENG I know it &apos;s my fault , I fell in love with Iveta , and I accept full responsibility , &quot; Josef concluded .

LANG_ENG Development of Trip Prices Since 1989
LANG_ENG Until 1989 , only five state travel agencies were allowed in the former Czechoslovakia: Čedok , Sporturist , CKM , Rekrea , and Autoturist .
LANG_ENG As travelling to the West was strictly limited , travel agencies of the time mostly sold tours to the socialist block countries .
LANG_ENG For their holiday , Czech tourists thus went to the sea to the German Democratic Republic; Soviet Union (Sochi , Crimea near the Black Sea); Bulgaria; Romania (both to the Black Sea); and Hungary (Balaton).
LANG_ENG The only exception was the period from 1962 to 1972 , when we had the opportunity to travel to Yugoslavia . Nevertheless , the Yugoslavian regime turned West , which caused significant limitations to trips to Yugoslavia for Czech tourists .
LANG_ENG A great paradox of the socialistic period was that citizens of the socialist block (i.e. Czechoslovaks too) were not allowed free individual travel within the socialist countries .
LANG_ENG If a Czechoslovak citizen wanted to travel , as an individual , to , for example , the Soviet Union or Poland , an invitation letter from the country was necessary; otherwise , individual travel was impossible .
LANG_ENG At the time , travel agencies would offer some trips to the West , but one either had to stand in a line overnight , with a sleeping bag or have some &quot; good friends &quot; in the agency .
LANG_ENG Still , that was not all .
LANG_ENG A foreign currency assurance was essential for travels to the West . It was not granted to politically unreliable people , who were not allowed to travel at all .
LANG_ENG Czechoslovakian currency was not freely convertible; without the currency assurance , it was not possible to obtain financial means (Western currency) for travelling West .
LANG_ENG Most often , Czechs spent their holiday at home , which resulted in great number of cottages and summer houses , a habit that survives until now .
LANG_ENG Since 1989 , Czech tourism thus experienced a real revolution .
LANG_ENG While until 1989 , a holiday in the GDR or Bulgaria was the climax of our travels , last year , Czechs spent 4.5 million holidays in countries all over the world .
LANG_ENG A great paradox we do not realise anymore is that until 1989 , we could not freely visit the currently most popular Croatia , as it was part of former Yugoslavia .
LANG_ENG Right at the beginning of 1990 , visa requirements for neighbouring West European countries were cancelled . This started a huge wave of short-term visits of chiefly Vienna and Germany .
LANG_ENG Czechoslovaks could not get enough of travelling to the West . Everyone wanted to go there for at least a moment .
LANG_ENG For example , in Paris , Czech tours slept in parks in tents , because their income at the time was not enough to pay for a hotel or a pension .
LANG_ENG A typical feature of Czech tourism then was bringing their own food (cans , salami , etc .) to save money .
LANG_ENG Another important moment was the introduction of freely convertible Czech Crown . After decades , our tourists thus finally able to freely buy Western currencies .
LANG_ENG Our living standards and average income were growing , which , around 1997 , resulted in another important moment .
LANG_ENG Since 1997 , increased demand allowed travel agencies to prepare regular trips by charter airlines . Compared to the past , air trips thus became unbelievably cheap due to the ability to order quantity discounts .
LANG_ENG By the end of 1990s , Czechs did not need visa for visiting nearly all developed world countries , except for the USA . This made our travelling even easier .
LANG_ENG The next significant event in the history of after revolution travelling came in 2000 . High demand resulted in the historically first direct charter flight from the Czech Republic to an exotic country , Thailand .
LANG_ENG Since then , direct charter flights take Czech tourists to warm exotic countries . This winter , flights from the Czech Republic will reach twelve exotic destinations .
LANG_ENG Currently about 100 thousand Czechs visit exotic countries every year !
LANG_ENG Yet another important event of this period , symbolising our development after the revolution , came in 2008 .
LANG_ENG On November 17 , 2008 , the USA removed visa requirements for Czech tourists . Our country has thus permanently joined the world &apos;s most developed countries .
LANG_ENG For the first time in history , in 2008 Czechs spent more than a half of their holidays abroad (50.3%); and for the first time in history , they spent over 15 thousand Crowns per person per holiday abroad , including their costs at the destination .
LANG_ENG General Meeting Should Find a President , Mate Threat Returns
LANG_ENG For nearly five months , Czech football has had no President . There exists a risk that Ivan Hašek &apos;s successor , the head of Czech Republic &apos;s Football Association (FAČR) will not be known even after another extraordinary general meeting , which is to take place in Nymburk on Thursday .
LANG_ENG There is still no agreement as to which election rules to follow .
LANG_ENG Without it , voting for the three candidates will not start .
LANG_ENG Jindřich Rajchl , Miroslav Pelta , and Tomáš Paclík are eager to lead Czech football .
LANG_ENG Hašek resigned from his function in June . When leaving , he called to his colleagues to unite and find a strong personality who would lead football in the future .
LANG_ENG However , Hašek &apos;s era sees football back in quarrels between both association chambers , unable to agree on a common candidate .
LANG_ENG This was fully shown on September 16 , when a new President was to be chosen .
LANG_ENG General meeting delegates wasted their trip to the National House in Prague , Smíchov , as the negotiations remained blocked , not just regarding the election method .
LANG_ENG No agreement was reached as to who is entitled to vote at the general meeting - whether the statutory representatives only , or also officials given power of attorney .
LANG_ENG This single point has been partially settled since , thanks to a recommendation of the Institute of State and Law , according to which representation based on power of attorney is not possible .
LANG_ENG Arguments concerning the election rules continue , though .
LANG_ENG The Executive Board has not been of much help either , though at its meetings , both regular and extraordinary , it is mostly preoccupied by this issue .
LANG_ENG The view of election options has changed several times , but the key point remains the same .
LANG_ENG The question is: How to proceed in the 3rd round to avoid mate ?
LANG_ENG &quot; The argument is based on whether to follow the by-laws or to find another model , &quot; says one of the three FAČR Vice-Presidents , Dušan Svoboda , who represents professional football in the association &apos;s management .
LANG_ENG Based on the model given by the by-laws , the winner of the 3rd round is a candidate with higher percentage support from the chamber he is the candidate for .
LANG_ENG Moravia is said to accept a compromise to have a candidate with the highest percentage of total votes from both chambers win the election .
LANG_ENG The Czech part stresses a condition that in the percentage total , the winner must gain at least two-third superiority .
LANG_ENG &quot; However , the two previous rounds would then lose their meaning; that would completely deny the two-chamber concept , &quot; Svoboda agrees with Moravia &apos;s arguments . He says it would be best not to bend the rules and vote according to the existing regulations .
LANG_ENG Somewhat surprisingly Tomáš Paclík agrees with his opinion even if it is estimated that the election rules defined by the by-laws fits Pelta best of the candidates .
LANG_ENG &apos;I wish the elections follow the by-laws to the maximum.&apos;
LANG_ENG &quot; I want to avoid all kinds of representative nonsense , as at the previous general meeting , &quot; says the owner of Viktorie Plzeň , who is a candidate for the first time; and in his statements he chiefly stood against Pelta .
LANG_ENG Pelta remains an optimist .
LANG_ENG He believes the new President will be known in Nymburk; he also hopes that in the future , the candidates will cooperate constructively .
LANG_ENG &quot; All passionate stirring will calm down with today &apos;s prospective advance of the national team into the European Championship . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; Football will be back on the happy wave , people will be more willing to cooperate , &quot; a Jablonec functionary says . Of the three candidates , he has the most experience with football management on both professional and regional levels .
LANG_ENG Rajchl is more reserved .
LANG_ENG &quot; I hope for an agreement , but the situation is very ambivalent . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; It is not between people from Bohemia and Moravia , but there are attempts at purposeful adjustment of regulations . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; That may cause another blockage of the general meeting . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; I hope the common sense wins , &quot; Rajchl said .
LANG_ENG There is not much time left for an agreement between the parties .
LANG_ENG Some negotiations are said to have taken place directly in Montenegro; but who knows if the football generality will be complete before the match .
LANG_ENG An extra flight that was to take , among others , the Vice Presidents Dalibor Kučera and Rajchl to Podgorica did not leave Prague in the morning due to a technical failure . An alternative was sought for in order to transport part of the executive board to the scene of the barraged rematch .
LANG_ENG Finally , a meeting at ministry level , said to happen on Wednesday , may decide .
LANG_ENG Minister of Education , Youth , and Sports , Josef Dobeš , would like to force the split parties inside the strongest sports association in the country to reach an agreement .
LANG_ENG A lot is in the game: Government grants; football trustworthiness; and the planned ČSTV general meeting dealing with new direction of Czech sports following Sazka &apos;s financial problems .
LANG_ENG Paclík Enters the Presidential Fight As He Cannot See a Suitable Candidate
LANG_ENG If , before the extraordinary general meeting , the Head of Pilsen football players , Tomáš Paclík , saw a strong candidate , who would meet all of his expectations of a new Football Association of the Czech Republic (FAČR) President , he would not even apply for the top function .
LANG_ENG &quot; If there was a good quality candidate , I &apos;d fight for him and not participate in the fight . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; But no such person has currently been found , &quot; Paclík said to ČTK .
LANG_ENG Paclík &apos;s motivation to join the fight with Miroslav Pelta and Jindřich Rajchl is to try to prevent Pelta , reportedly the favourite of the elections , from entering the top of the FAČR .
LANG_ENG Moreover , Paclík emphasizes that should he win , he would only remain the President until 2013 , when a regular general meeting is scheduled .
LANG_ENG In the future , he would like to see the position given to an experienced top manager , not excessively connected to football life .
LANG_ENG &quot; I &apos;ve spoken to some people that could be considered . &quot;

LANG_ENG &quot; I &apos;d like to change this opinion , &quot; he said .

Berber is a man of controversial reputation , who is , behind the scenes , known as powerful lobbyist , capable of influencing the votes of general meeting delegates .

LANG_ENG &quot; If he wins , current situation will be preserved and nothing in football would move forward . &quot;

LANG_ENG He is hinting at the fact that some years ago , Pelta &apos;s name was recorded during phone tapping in a corruption affair investigation; Pelta came out without a sentence .

LANG_ENG &quot; He (Pelta) would be the first one I &apos;d go to . &quot;

LANG_ENG &quot; I don &apos;t poke my nose in what I don &apos;t understand either , &apos; said Paclík , who gained a lot of attention in September , when he supported the removal of board of referees , led by Luděk Macela , replaced by Dagmar Damková .

LANG_ENG Pelta Promised New FAČR Regulations That Would Avoid Election Mate
LANG_ENG Two days before the general meeting of the football association , one of the Presidential candidates , Miroslav Pelta , promised that if he is elected , he would strive for new FAČR regulations to avoid future disputes over the election rules .

LANG_ENG Europe &apos;s most beautiful pools
LANG_ENG Leap into the water
LANG_ENG By Julia Stanek
LANG_ENG Paddling pools with universal fibre optics and status pools in Budapest . Travellers can experience Europe &apos;s incredible water - and relax tired limbs in a Jacuzzi after a city tour or a ramble .
LANG_ENG One book can tell you where the water is at its best .
LANG_ENG There was one thing Iris Meder could not do without on research trips over the last one and a half years: her swimming costume .
LANG_ENG Lying back on the water , she has looked up at artistically designed domes , has swum towards marble cherubs awaiting her at the edge of the pool and has marvelled at meticulously restored art nouveau swimming pools .
LANG_ENG She rushed to add any pool she liked to her notebook - with essential details on the construction and the history of the building .
LANG_ENG The architectural historian Meder looked at more than 200 swimming pools - and has now compiled here experiences in her recently published book Badefreuden (The Joys of Bathing), covering everything from public swimming baths in Munich to historical bathing palaces in the Black Forest and &quot; hardcore concrete buildings &quot; in Taunus .
LANG_ENG Her &quot; journey to the most unusual baths in Central Europe &quot; took here through 13 countries . Besides Germany , Austria and Switzerland , she visited baths in Italy , France , the Czech Republic , Slovakia , Slovenia , Hungary , Romania and Poland - and one city each in Luxembourg , Serbia and Croatia .
LANG_ENG The 46-year-old is a real bathing culture enthusiast .
LANG_ENG She has very little enthusiasm for sport , says Meder - but in the water , it &apos;s a different matter .
LANG_ENG The only downside is that fans of swimming have to cope with blue glazed tiles and the stench of chlorine while joggers can breathe in the beguiling scent of spruce forests or listen to the bright twittering of birds in the park .
LANG_ENG &quot; One day , I asked myself why swimming baths always have to be so ugly , &quot; says Vienna-based Meder .
LANG_ENG &quot; So I started collecting beautiful baths . &quot;
LANG_ENG Water surface doubles architecture
LANG_ENG Splashing in the diving pool and ethereal sauna oils - the wellness factor in baths is so great because all the senses are stimulated , according to Meder .
LANG_ENG And swimming baths can be a real treat for the eyes if the builders have gone to the trouble . &quot; You have the surface of the water in pools instead of a floor . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; The surface is very transparent , but also reflects the beauty of the entire building . &quot;
LANG_ENG Everything is mirrored visually: high ceilings , colourful tiles and diving boards .
LANG_ENG The illustrated pocketbook The Joys of Bathing provides valuable information on the architectural and cultural history of historic pleasure and health oases over 190 pages - and makes you want to leap into the water .
LANG_ENG Pool collector Meder discovered some notable examples during research in Hungary .
LANG_ENG She found nitrate-rich water in a karst cave (the Cave Bath in Miskolctapolca) and a thermal bath filled with alkaline water in a bottle-shaped building (Városi Termálfürdö in Jászberény) in addition to magnificent therapeutic baths such as the 100-year-old Széchenyi baths in Budapest .
LANG_ENG Many of the heated outdoor baths in Switzerland and Austria , on the other hand , offer spectacular views . You can view all of Zurich from a rooftop bath or look out on the snow-capped Arlberg from an outdoor pool in St. Anton . And there is a window in the steam bath giving a view of the action on the ski piste .
LANG_ENG Perhaps the most unusual pool design awaits bathers in Längenfeld . The Aqua Dome in Ötztal looks like a UFO has just landed in the Alps .
LANG_ENG It steams during the winter from three open-topped shells dwarfed by the Ötztal mountains behind it .
LANG_ENG Alhambra in the Black Forest
LANG_ENG Pool collector Meder was not greeted by the smell of chlorine in every swimming pool .
LANG_ENG A lot of thermal baths smell of sulphur . The Árpád baths in Békescsaba , Hungary , smell so strongly of oil you may find it difficult to believe you are in a health spa .
LANG_ENG The smell comes from the hydrogen carbonate in the alkaline water . The water is almost black with silt that sticks to the skin as soon as you slide into the pool - a wellness experience of a particular kind .
LANG_ENG Iris Meder , however , was at one point disappointed in her search for beautiful bathing places . When she tried to visit the outdoor pool at the Czech baths of Luhatschowitz , she found the area sealed off .
LANG_ENG The baths , designed by the architect Dušan Jurkovic in 1902 , have been closed .
LANG_ENG When Meder looked through the weather-beaten windows of the red , white and yellow art nouveau building , she could see weeds growing up through the tiles .
LANG_ENG One place where decay has been stopped in its tracks is a magical swimming bath in the Black Forest - the Palais Thermal in Bad Wildbad .
LANG_ENG The baths have already gone through three stages of construction . You will not only discover neo-Romanesque elements from the period after it was built in 1844 , but also a Moorish hall in Alhambra style added around 1900 .
LANG_ENG Following its careful modernisation in 1995 , the Palais Thermal is the favourite swimming pool of pool connoisseur Iris Meder - and not just because she comes from the Black Forest .
LANG_ENG &quot; It is a real achievement to harmonise such different architectural styles so brilliantly , &quot; says Meder .
LANG_ENG A dip in the thermal pool in such a palace is clearly of secondary importance .
LANG_ENG Agricultural commodities speculation
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bank has commodity trading investigated
LANG_ENG By Christian Teevs
LANG_ENG Will Deutsche Bank stop trading agricultural commodities ?
LANG_ENG According to SPIEGEL ONLINE , Josef Ackermann has given a working group the task of investigating the consequences of speculation for the poor around the world .
LANG_ENG The CEO plans to make changes in January .
LANG_ENG Hamburg -
LANG_ENG For German citizens the situation is clear . According to one study , 84 percent of Germans find it unacceptable that banks speculate on agricultural commodities such as wheat and maize .
LANG_ENG Two thirds of those questioned demand that Deutsche Bank and other banks cease trading in agricultural commodities , as trading deepens the problems faced by the very poorest people around the world .
LANG_ENG The findings were made in a survey conducted by the Forsa Institute for Social Research and Statistical Analysis on behalf of the consumer organisation Foodwatch .
LANG_ENG The study is based on a report presented by Foodwatch in mid-October .
LANG_ENG The author of the report , Harald Schumann , shows that betting on global commodities exchanges drives up prices - and the banks are therefore complicit in global hunger .
LANG_ENG The campaign by consumer advocates is directed specifically at the head of Deutsche Bank , Josef Ackermann , although large banking houses such as Goldman Sachs and Morgan Stanley trade in the same way .
LANG_ENG Originally , commodity betting was designed as a means of protecting traders against price fluctuations .
LANG_ENG However , most experts now agree that the gamblers have left behind the rules of supply and demand - and are profiting at the expense of the poorest .
LANG_ENG In contrast to US competitors , Ackermann has responded to the criticism . He has promised to investigate the accusations and has said that no trade is &quot; worth putting Deutsche Bank &apos;s good reputation at risk . &quot;
LANG_ENG According to SPIEGEL ONLINE , an international working group is currently investigating the accusations contained in the Foodwatch report .
LANG_ENG The investigation should be complete by the end of the year when the findings will be presented to Deutsche Bank &apos;s board of managing directors - with recommendations for action .
LANG_ENG The head of the bank then plans to announce changes following the investigation at the end of January .
LANG_ENG Commodities trading may be reduced or stopped completely .
LANG_ENG Ackermann working on his image
LANG_ENG The president of Foodwatch , Thilo Bode , welcomed the news while emphasising his criticism of the financial sector . &quot; Betting on rising food prices is an extreme example of how thoughtlessly banks are currently acting against the common interest . &quot;
LANG_ENG As top bank lobbyist , Ackermann has a particular duty , according to Bode .
LANG_ENG &quot; Deutsche Bank must remove all investments from its portfolio that bet money on food prices , &quot; said Bode .
LANG_ENG &quot; It does not matter whether this is about starving people or the reputation of Deutsche Bank . &quot;
LANG_ENG Ackermann &apos;s sensitive response is at first surprising , but then the CEO would like to present a perfect image just a few months before the end of his term in office .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bank announced on Monday that the chairman will not move to the supervisory board as had been planned .
LANG_ENG Cancelling contentious food commodity speculation could improve his image .
LANG_ENG He also need have little concern for the costs - it would be up to his successor to manage the outcome .
LANG_ENG One in two people would withdraw commodities investments
LANG_ENG Foodwatch is striving to keep up the pressure on the manager .
LANG_ENG To date , more than 30,000 internet users have joined the organisation &apos;s campaign .
LANG_ENG Bode published the survey on Tuesday . The survey was conducted for the Forsa Institute for Social Research and Statistical Analysis on 7 and 8 November and 1001 people took part .
LANG_ENG No more than eleven percent think it is legitimate for Deutsche Bank to offer investments that bet on the price of foodstuffs .
LANG_ENG Many banking customers would also take direct action if they discover that their bank is involved in such trading . According to the survey , one in two would withdraw investments that end up in commodities speculation .
LANG_ENG 43 percent would recommend leaving the bank , 49 percent said they would think about closing their account and switching to a different bank .
LANG_ENG 21er Haus in Vienna
LANG_ENG The relocated pavilion
LANG_ENG By Ingeborg Wiensowski
LANG_ENG An architectural history with highs , lows and a happy-ever-after . Austria &apos;s Pavilion for the 1958 World &apos;s Fair in Brussels won prizes , became a museum in Vienna , stood empty and was abandoned .
LANG_ENG Now it is being reopened as an exhibition centre .
LANG_ENG Austria &apos;s pavilion , designed by Karl Schwanzer for the 1958 Brussels World &apos;s Fair , is a famous textbook example of modern post-war architecture with its clear shapes , glass halls , bold strokes and the new construction materials that expressed belief in technical progress .
LANG_ENG Schwanzer &apos;s pavilion won the Grand Prix d &apos;Architecture in 1958 for its light floating steel-glass structure .
LANG_ENG The building is considered a milestone in contemporary architecture .
LANG_ENG It made the architect so famous that he also built Austria &apos;s pavilion at the next world &apos;s fair .
LANG_ENG He finally shot to fame internationally in 1973 with his legendary four-cylinder BMW Tower and its bowl-shaped sister building .
LANG_ENG The pavilion , planned as a temporary exhibition building , was relocated to the Schweizer Garten near Vienna &apos;s Südbahnhof , converted and opened as the Museum of the 20th Century in 1962 - and is widely referred to as the &quot; 20er Haus &quot; for this reason .
LANG_ENG However , the building was not suitable as a museum for technical and spatial reasons - it had no walls to hang artworks and poor air conditioning .
LANG_ENG Nonetheless , it continued to be used until contemporary art in Vienna was given a new home .
LANG_ENG The building stood empty from 2001 and fell into a worse and worse state of repair .
LANG_ENG The architect Adolf Krischanitz has now renovated the pavilion , which has been named the &quot; 21er Haus &quot; and will be used as a contemporary art museum .
LANG_ENG The museum is a branch of the Belvedere museum , which will open the first exhibition on Tuesday evening - a delight in every respect .
LANG_ENG Agnes Husslein-Arco who became the new director of the Austrian Galerie Belvedere in 2007 was instrumental in the new beginning .
LANG_ENG Husslein-Arco , an art history graduate with a remarkable career in her youth as an ice skater , who went on to Sotheby &apos;s , the Guggenheim Museum and to become the founding director of the Museum der Moderne in Salzburg , convinced politicians and conservators to go ahead with renovation , attracted public funding and private sponsorship and decided on the use of the building .
LANG_ENG The new museum was to house the Fritz Wotruba Foundation &apos;s permanent collection , a café and a bookshop alongside contemporary art . An office building was also to be built .
LANG_ENG Strict supervision &amp; limited budget
LANG_ENG Krischanitz was then the ideal choice to carry out the project .
LANG_ENG He was known , of course , for having renovated and expanded Joseph Olbrich &apos;s Secession in Vienna , and had won the competition , but he also studied under Schwanzer at the Vienna University of Technology and the pavilion was an &quot; exceptionally important place &quot; for him where had visited exhibitions &quot; almost every weekend . &quot;
LANG_ENG He knew the original design and knew the issues the building was facing , a building that had already lost some of its grandeur and lightness when it was relocated to Vienna and converted .
LANG_ENG The problems facing the latest alterations were much greater . The building was &quot; an energy guzzler , &quot; says Krischanitz .
LANG_ENG The window profiles of the glass facade were replaced , fibreglass-reinforced safety glass was put in and the glass roof was replaced by high-grade safety glass .
LANG_ENG Thermal bridge steel girders were strengthened or replaced and asbestos was removed from ceilings .
LANG_ENG Two lower floors created space for the new use of the building , a sunken light well between the building and the street provides lighting , a bridge leads to the entrance - almost a new building , but still the delicate Schwanzer pavilion .
LANG_ENG The original external doors have been retained and the building has been painted in the old red-brown colour of rust-proofing .
LANG_ENG And the cinema hall is exactly as it used to be .
LANG_ENG All this under the strict supervision of the monument authority and with a limited budget .
LANG_ENG &quot; We often had to find a material that was good , cheap and met with the approval of the monument authority , &quot; says Krischanitz , pointing to the rough flooring in the basement .
LANG_ENG The building has remained flexible and light despite the constraints , problems and conversions .
LANG_ENG Krischanitz stated recently that the pavilion &quot; from Brussels &quot; had been tough - a typical &quot; drop in the city &quot; story .
LANG_ENG Architecture like this is &quot; always in the wrong place &quot; and nonetheless wants to &quot; stimulate a real awareness . &quot;
LANG_ENG The 21er Haus is very much in the right place , as there has been a stroke of luck in town planning . The completely redesigned &quot; main station quarter &quot; with offices and residential properties is developing around the Schweizer Garten .
LANG_ENG There may also be a second stroke of luck . The 21er Haus may be bolstered by another Krischanitz building - the collector Francesca von Habsburg has purchased the Temporäre Kunsthalle Berlin and is reported to be negotiating with the city for a neighbouring location in the Schweizer Garten .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bahn plans winter crisis package into the millions
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bahn has come up with a crisis plan to prevent train cancellations in the winter .
LANG_ENG The number of employees is to double .
LANG_ENG The costs will run into the millions .
LANG_ENG According to a newspaper report , Deutsche Bahn will spend more than 70 million Euros more this year in the battle to prevent winter-time cancellations and delays .
LANG_ENG Referring to an internal crisis plan at Deutsche Bahn , the Bild newspaper has reported that investment of around 300 million Euros in total is planned up to 2015 .
LANG_ENG Investment is intended to improve the availability of locomotives and the rail network , even in the face of extreme weather conditions .
LANG_ENG The number of internal and external employees involved in removing snow from rail facilities and platforms is to double to 16,000 .
LANG_ENG The aim is to clear platforms of snow and ice by start of business and 90 percent of the critical points within four to five hours .
LANG_ENG Rüdiger Grube , head of Deutsche Bahn , warned of train cancellations and delays this winter at a summit with government and industry two months ago .
LANG_ENG Last winter , Deutsche Bahn had considerable difficulties in its passenger business , as it lacked reserves in the face of difficult weather conditions .
LANG_ENG Numerous new regional trains have been waiting for years for approval from the Federal Railway Office .
LANG_ENG There is also some delay in the delivery of ICE trains .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bahn has also been forced to have the axles of ICE trains checked significantly more frequently for many years , after an ICE train &apos;s axle broke in Cologne &apos;s main station .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bank pays multi-million pound fine in the USA
LANG_ENG Fresh trouble is following hard on the heels of the uproar around Josef Ackermann , CEO of Deutsche Bank: Deutsche Bank faces a multi-million pound fine in the USA .
LANG_ENG As if the problems at home were not already enough for Deutsche Bank , the industry giant &apos;s past in the USA is now also catching up with it . Frankfurt-based Deutsche Bank will pay 145 million dollars (106 million Euros) to settle disputes arising from the bankruptcy of five major credit unions during the financial crisis .
LANG_ENG The issue centres on the sale of mortgage securities .
LANG_ENG The National Credit Union Administration (NCUA), a financial market regulator , accuses a string of major banks of having used false promises to mislead credit unions into buying the financial products .
LANG_ENG The value of the securities dropped dramatically during the financial crisis and brought down the credit unions .
LANG_ENG &quot; We are happy to have resolved the issue without the parties going to court , &quot; said a Deutsche Bank spokesman in new York .
LANG_ENG The bank did not admit culpability in the settlement .
LANG_ENG The same is true of Citigroup , which agreed to pay 20.5 million dollars .
LANG_ENG The NCUA chairman , Debbie Matz , welcomed the responsiveness of the two banks .
LANG_ENG The National Credit Union Administration (NCUA) is responsible for the US credit unions and intervenes in bankruptcies to protect customer deposits .
LANG_ENG The NCUA is fighting for compensation for losses that run into the billions .
LANG_ENG The current settlements are the first of their kind .
LANG_ENG The regulator had also approached other major banks and sued JPMorgan Chase , the Royal Bank of Scotland and Goldman Sachs in the summer .
LANG_ENG The dubious mortgage securities are so-called mortgage-backed securities .
LANG_ENG They are underpinned by home loans .
LANG_ENG This sealed the fate of a number of financial companies when the US property bubble exploded in 2007 .
LANG_ENG The US investment bank , Lehman Brothers , went belly up in September 2008 at the height of the financial crisis .
LANG_ENG The banks battling against a strong wind in the USA several years later .
LANG_ENG Investors and regulators have brought a vast number of claims for compensation or to punish misconduct .
LANG_ENG The Federal Housing Finance Agency (FHFA) has been behind the largest wave of claims .
LANG_ENG It accuses 18 major international banks of having taken in US lenders Fannie Mae and Freddie Mac on mortgage transactions valued at around 200 billion dollars .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bank also faces legal action by the FHFA covering multiple transactions with a total value of 14.2 billion dollars from 2005 to 2007 .
LANG_ENG The regulator is demanding that the Frankfurt-based bank take responsibility for &quot; substantial losses , &quot; but has not yet specified the exact sum .
LANG_ENG Deutsche Bank has rejected the claims as baseless and has declared its intention to fend off the claims .
LANG_ENG Warren Buffett pumps 10 billion into IBM
LANG_ENG Financial guru Buffett is investing heavily in the IT company , IBM .
LANG_ENG Since March , he has bought up shares totalling more than ten billion dollars .
LANG_ENG Until now , the major American investor , Warren Buffett , had always claimed not to invest in IT and computing companies , as it was difficult to forecast the long-term development .
LANG_ENG However , IBM &apos;s annual reports changed his mind on investing in the industry .
LANG_ENG According to Buffett , he should have realised much earlier that IBM primarily offers services and purchases computer systems for the IT departments of other companies .
LANG_ENG Investment by Warren Buffett is considered a knighthood in the financial world .
LANG_ENG The IT veteran IBM has now earned the title of &quot; Sir IBM . &quot;
LANG_ENG Buffett revealed that he had purchased IBM shares totalling 10.7 billion dollars since March on the US business news broadcaster CNBC .
LANG_ENG His investment holding company , Berkshire Hathaway , has become one of the largest shareholders in IBM with a 5.5 percent stake .

LANG_ENG He praised the management , which has managed to bring in profits even during the economic crisis .
LANG_ENG &quot; They have done a great job , &quot; said Buffett , referring to the management strategy .
LANG_ENG For a fairly long time , IBM has focused on lucrative IT services such as data centres .
LANG_ENG The computer pioneer - now more than 100 years old - also provides software and consultancy services , as well as powerful business computers .
LANG_ENG Buffett had avoided technology firms to date .
LANG_ENG He claimed only to invest in companies whose business he understands
LANG_ENG and invested in a freight railway , for example , a lubricant manufacturer and a machine manufacturer .
LANG_ENG His holding company , Berkshire Hathaway , owns shares in a long list of major companies such as Coca-Cola and Munich Re (formerly Münchener Rück) alongside around 80 of its own subsidiaries .
LANG_ENG The 81-year-old took over the small textile company Berkshire Hathaway in the 1960s and built it up , with clever investments , into one of the most valuable companies in the world .
LANG_ENG His lifestyle , however , has remained humble ,
LANG_ENG making him a cult figure for countless investors around the world .
LANG_ENG His almost infallible instinct for making money has earned him a nickname as the &quot; Oracle from Omaha . &quot;
LANG_ENG The IBM share price rose by one percent before the markets opened following the announcement of Buffett &apos;s investment .
LANG_ENG &quot; Big Blue , &quot; as IBM is also known , is worth more than 220 billion dollars on the stock exchange , making it one of the most valuable technology companies in the world alongside Apple and Microsoft .

LANG_ENG The founder , Bill Gates , is a close friend .
LANG_ENG Imminent danger
LANG_ENG Following the discovery of the &quot; Zwickau cell , &quot; Turkish media express doubt about the rule of law in Germany .

LANG_ENG The murder of eight Turkish and one Greek businessman between 2000 and 2006 was the result of right-wing extremist ideology .
LANG_ENG Fear and concern has been the reaction to this report in Turkey and within the German-Turkish community in Germany .
LANG_ENG For many German Turks , the news brings back to life a long-dead spectre . There has been no comparable right-wing extremist violence against Turks since the arson attacks in Mölln in November 1992 and in Solingen in May 1993 .
LANG_ENG There was never any question , however , that xenophobia does exist in Germany .
LANG_ENG The right-wing extremist network that has now been discovered , however , is on a scale that has not yet been fully understood .
LANG_ENG &quot; Is this a revival of the bloody ideology ? &quot; was the headline of the internet edition of the Turkish newspaper Haberturk .

LANG_ENG The coverage by some Turkish media has been like a slap in the face . &quot; Germany &apos;s present on the fiftieth anniversary &quot; is the title of one article on the Haber X Turkish internet platform , which comments on the circumstances around the series of murders .

LANG_ENG The behaviour of the police and the subsequently successful manhunt is heavily criticised on German-Turkish internet forums .

LANG_ENG The photo of the burnt out ruin of Solingen is deeply engrained in German and Turkish memory .
LANG_ENG No other event has shown the Turks living here more clearly that there is imminent danger and shown the Germans that mistrust and distance can culminate in real violence .
LANG_ENG The attacks , however , increased the sense of Turkish unity .
