LANG_ENG The North Stream , a new portal for the entry of Russian gas into Europe
LANG_ENG The North Stream gasduct connecting Western Europe and Russia directly along the bottom of the Baltic sea , has been commissioned .
LANG_ENG It is scheduled to supply gas for the equivalent of 30 million homes .
LANG_ENG Gazprom , the giant Russian gas producer , wanted to celebrate the event with a &quot; bang . &quot;
LANG_ENG Over 500 guests including four heads of State and of government took part last Tuesday on the shores of the Baltic , between an orchestral performance and a fine buffet , in the inauguration of North Stream , the new gasduct , which directly links Russia and Germany under the sea .
LANG_ENG Symbolically , the German Chancellor Angela Merkel , the Russian president Dmitri Medvedev , the French prime minister François Fillon and his Dutch opposite number Mark Rutte jointly turned the valve controlling the entry of Russian gas into the West European network .
LANG_ENG With this new gasduct , 27,5 thousand million additional cubic metres of Russian gas will arrive every year in Western Europe via a first pipeline of 1 224 km linking the region of Saint Petersburg to the Land of Mecklemburg-Pomerania .
LANG_ENG A second pipeline is due to be ready by the end of 2012 , making it possible to deliver a total of 55 thousand million cubic metres of gas , the equivalent of the entire French consumption .
LANG_ENG And the possibility of constructing a third pipeline of the same course is already under discussion .
LANG_ENG For Gazprom , the completion on time of this huge project is a victory .
LANG_ENG The project was fiercely competed for by Poland and the Baltic States .
LANG_ENG The North Stream will in fact allow gas to be delivered directly to Germany , avoiding any passage via a third country (Poland or the Ukraine).
LANG_ENG These two countries will lose some of their power: it will become more difficult for them to influence Russia by threatening to close access to West European markets .
LANG_ENG At the most critical point of the debate , Warsaw did not hesitate to compare North Stream new &quot; German-Soviet pact , &quot; referring to the alliance between Hitler and Stalin to occupy Poland in 1939 .
LANG_ENG That is to say that the topic is politically sensitive .
LANG_ENG By supporting this Russian project , Western Europe is gaining greater security for its supplies .
LANG_ENG But at the price of depriving Europe of energy , since the project has created a breach between eastern and western Europe .
LANG_ENG Russia has succeeded in less than five years , in achieving its vision of a direct alliance between Russia and the the rich Western countries , which consume large quantities of gas , and whose deposits are declining .
LANG_ENG &quot; This gasduct is a component of partnership with Russia , it is a new artery which links us organically , &quot; confirmed François Fillon inaugurating the gasduct , demonstrating to what extent large gas contracts are both politically and economically important .
LANG_ENG All this explains the broad smiles on the faces of the heads of Gazprom , present in large numbers at Lubmin , the point of arrival of the gas .
LANG_ENG The construction of this gasduct is also a technical exploit .
LANG_ENG The undersea pipeline is made of steel embedded in concrete , in order to protect it from ships &apos; anchors .
LANG_ENG Ir rests on the bottom of the sea , at an average depth of 200 metres .
LANG_ENG To construct it , it was necessary to avoid minefields dating back to the second World War .
LANG_ENG &quot; A hundred had to be removed or destroyed as a precaution , &quot; says Jens Müller , spokesman of North Stream company .
LANG_ENG It was also necessary to multiply steps of protecting the fauna and the flora .
LANG_ENG The pipeline is a long metal serpent , of weight equivalent to that of 242 Eiffel towers , with no breaks throughout its length , no valves and no maintenance stations .
LANG_ENG A control platform was provided on the level of Sweden , but the project managers abandoned it since the Swedes were not keen on seeing a Russian State company becoming permanently on its shores .
LANG_ENG &quot; In case of accident we stop the passage of gas for at least one minute , &quot; states Jens Müller .
LANG_ENG In the case of a leak , the gas contained in the gasduct therefore escapes into the air .
LANG_ENG But this is thought to be unlikely by the constructors who provided welds to leak only every 100 000 years .
LANG_ENG The surveillance of the state of the gasduct is provided by an undersea robot , pulled by a ship for outside observation , as well as by an apparatus circulating within the gasduct .
LANG_ENG Being cigar-shaped , it is introduced inside the 1-metre wide pipeline , and it is pushed along by the gas .
LANG_ENG On arrival after 3 complete days of travel at a speed of 3 metres per second , it delivers precise information concerning any metal deformation .
LANG_ENG The gasduct was designed to work for 50 years without any need for even the smallest repair .
LANG_ENG The gas circulation is implemented simply by its pressure .
LANG_ENG This is 200 bar on leaving and 100 bar on arrival .
LANG_ENG Five companies combined their forces to implement this project .
LANG_ENG The leader remains Gazprom , which holds 51% of the shareholding .
LANG_ENG The others are the German companies E.ON and BASF (15.5% each) and the Dutch Gasunie and the French Group GDF Suez (9% each).
LANG_ENG These five companies have created a joint enterprise called North Stream , delegated to construct and to operate the gasduct .
LANG_ENG It has its headquarters at Zug in Switzerland , where taxation is particularly favourable .
LANG_ENG Gazprom next leased to this company for twenty renewable years , the entire capacity of gas transport .
LANG_ENG &quot; Gazprom will pay for the total capacity , whatever may be the quantity of gas actually transported , &quot; states Jens Müller .
LANG_ENG The financing of the construction of the gasduct was provided to the extent of 30% by the shareholders and of 70% by Bank loans .
LANG_ENG The total cost of the works will be 7.4 thousand million Euros for the two pipelines .
LANG_ENG The GDF Suez investment will be about 240 millions .
LANG_ENG But the minority shareholders are certain to recover their costs , since Gazprom assumes the entire risk .
LANG_ENG The gasduct emerges from the Baltic sea at Lubmin on a sandy littoral planted with conifers .
LANG_ENG 4.5 metre high valves form the gas exit .
LANG_ENG Sensors measure pressure , temperature and the specific gravities of arriving gas before being transferred into German gasducts .
LANG_ENG Since last Tuesday , the terminal has been receiving one million cubic metres of Russian gas every hour .
LANG_ENG At full capacity , this will be 3 million an hour and in 2012 , 6 million .
LANG_ENG Moleskine , a brand card .
LANG_ENG Created fifteen years ago by an Italian company , Moleskine will restore the taste of writing .
LANG_ENG It is a scent of adventure , of hours sent in writing by a the light of a candle .
LANG_ENG The Moleskine notebook is easily recognised , by its black rectangular cover , its elastic , its broken white pages , as if aged over time .
LANG_ENG Nevertheless , the Moleskine notebook as we know it today , was born in 1997 .
LANG_ENG The Italian company Modo Modo , based in Milan , decided to launch a designer notebook .
LANG_ENG Maria Sebregondi , then a consultant of the company , has assumed responsibility for the launch of the new product .
LANG_ENG The notebook draws its inspiration from an old production technique , the mole skin which means varnished cotton used for covering benches , for example .
LANG_ENG This type of notebook is said to be highly prized by writers and travellers .
LANG_ENG &quot; Moleskine has been updated to meet current taste for an old and forgotten object , which was an avantgarde artists &apos; icon up to the XXth century , &quot; related Maria Sebregondi , who has since become the manager of the brand name at Modo Modo .
LANG_ENG Success is there .
LANG_ENG Between 2006 and 2010 , sales rose by 25% to reach 12.7 million units .
LANG_ENG One has travelled far from the production of the first years , when only 3000 notebooks were made .
LANG_ENG Moleskine is crossing the Italian frontiers and is exporting to 70 countries , from France to the USA .
LANG_ENG It is difficult to establish a profile of the typical purchaser , because the notebook attracts equally a businessman , a student and a professional .
LANG_ENG Moleskine consumers are cosmopolitan , open-minded and cultivated .
LANG_ENG The small Italian company , which had only 12 employees at the start , now has almost 100 and two offices , one in Milan and the other in New York .
LANG_ENG Its distributes its notebooks to Fnac libraries , small shops in town centres and has succeeded in becoming well known .
LANG_ENG &quot; We followed the spirit of the times and this need for new means of writing , notwithstanding the rise of e-mail , &quot; explains Maria Sebregondi .
LANG_ENG This cultural signature accompanies the development of Moleskine; recently , the brand launched an exhibition &quot; Detour &quot; where architects or artists exhibit their own notebook .
LANG_ENG In August , it also launched a leopardskin pattern cover on the occasion of the Film Festival in Locarno .
LANG_ENG Exploiting its success and the cultural aura , Moleskine diversified its products to include handbags , pens , computer bags . The brand includes every kind of support .
LANG_ENG A success , which aroused envy; in the autumn of 2006 , Modo Modo was bought by the investment fund SG Capital Europe , now Syntegra Capital , to write a new page in the history of Moleskine .
LANG_ENG Why is the rate of unemployment of handicapped workers so high ?
LANG_ENG Some 19% of handicapped persons are looking for work .
LANG_ENG The 15th week for the employment of the handicapped starts today .
LANG_ENG Despite a public voluntary policy introduced in 2005 , the rate of unemployment of the handicapped is still twice as high as the average , namely 19% , versus 9% for the population as a whole .
LANG_ENG Discouraging ?
LANG_ENG &quot; No , stresses Eric Blanchet , Director-General of Adapt , the association which organises the week for the employment of the handicapped . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; The progress achieved since 15 years ago is considerable . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; At that time the rate of unemployment was not 2x but 3x as high . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; There is however still a huge amount to do . &quot;
LANG_ENG It must be said that for the handicapped , the obstacles to obtaining employment are still many .
LANG_ENG They are rather old: 37% are over 50 (17% on average).
LANG_ENG They have rather a low level of qualifications; 80% do not have the &quot; bac &quot; and out of the 2.3 million students in higher education only 10 000 are handicapped .
LANG_ENG Lastly , long-term unemployment is very widespread , being 85% for the handicapped versus 38% on an average .
LANG_ENG Briefly , all these are criteria which greatly complicate a return to employment and which constitute the nub of the problem , &quot; according to Christian Grapin , director-general of Tremplin , an association created in 1992 to help companies to recruit handicapped workers .
LANG_ENG Here are some of the brakes .
LANG_ENG It is hardly necessary to speak about mentalities , which do change , but too slowly .
LANG_ENG A study carried out in April by the association IMS-Entreprendre pour la Cité showed that the managers questioned had a low level of knowledge of handicap , &quot; with an &quot; over-representation of persons in wheelchairs , psychically or intellectually deficient persons . &quot;
LANG_ENG Result - private companies employing over 20 persons are still far from achieving the objective of employing the 6% of handicapped workers , fixed by a law dating back to 1987 .
LANG_ENG The latter known figures dating to 2008 have a ratio of 2.6% .
LANG_ENG &quot; We are now on around 3% , &quot; says Pierre Blanc , director-general of the Agefiph , the organisation responsible for collecting contributions from companies which do not observe this law .
LANG_ENG Proof: The number of &quot; taxed &quot; establishments , like the sums paid , have fallen between 2007 and 2011 , from 59 000 to 46 000 structures (and from 606 to 480 million Euros).
LANG_ENG &quot; The law of 2005 , which raised the contributions , created a strong pressure on companies , explains Pierre Blanc . &quot;
LANG_ENG &quot; But this improvement also reflects a rise of consciousness , in particular within large groups . &quot;
LANG_ENG According to the ministry of employment , only 59% of establishments employing between 20 and 49 handicapped persons , versus 82% of companies employing between 100 and 199 persons .

LANG_ENG Before facing the Blues on Tuesday evening (20.45 hrs) Eden Hazard and Georges Leekens did not hide the pleasure , which this friendly match gave to them .

LANG_ENG &quot; You will realise this during the matches to come . Including that against France .
LANG_ENG Portugal is very confident
LANG_ENG The Portugal of Paulo Bento starts its return match against Bosnia (22h00) very optimistically , this Tuesday in Lisbon .
LANG_ENG On their way there , both teams appeared to lack realism .
LANG_ENG &quot; At the end of these 90 minutes , we will be a happy team and most importantly , a happy country . &quot;
LANG_ENG Paulo Bento already sees himself in Poland and in the Ukraine .
LANG_ENG For him there is not a shadow of a doubt , the Selection , with which he has been at odds since September 2010 , will qualify for Euro 2012 .
LANG_ENG Portugal is only 90 minutes away from happiness .
LANG_ENG But there is match to play and an opponent , Bosnia to conquer .
LANG_ENG In view of the (0-0), on Friday in the hell of Zenica it is clear that the games are not over .

LANG_ENG But on their side , in their illuminated Stade de la Luz in Lisbon , the Portuguese are convinced that they are playing in front of a public which must be enthusiastic , even if the match is very close , &quot; said an optimistic , but lucid , Bento
